27-30 Match Point Decklists
===========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on November 11, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff















[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20190318171748im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/mtg/files/Arena_Banner_850x90_1.jpg)![](https://web.archive.org/web/20190318171749im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/mtg/files/Arena_Banner_300x90_0.jpg)![](https://web.archive.org/web/20190318171749im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/mtg/files/Arena_Banner_748x90_0.jpg)](https://magic.wizards.com/en/mtgarena?utm_source=MTGArena&utm_medium=Banner&utm_campaign=1358606)

Two player finished with 30 (10-0) points in the Standard portion of Pro Tour *Guilds of Ravnica*, two finished with 27 points (9-1), one finished with 25 points (8-1-1), and 18 finished with 24 points (8-2).


30 Points (10-0) or 27 Points (9-1)
===================================







#### Gauthier, Guillaume - Mono-Blue Tempo
